2a1(rgyud): ar ra/ na
2a2(rgyud): nam sang gi

3a1(rgyud): rnams kyi mchog/ dpa' bo 'jig
3a2(rgyud): rten gsum las rgyal// rdo rje dbang phyug bsang ba'i rgya
3a3(rgyud): pad ma dkar po rgyas 'dra'i sran// pad ma rgyas 'di'i
3b1(rgyud): zhal mnga' ba// rang gi lag gi rdo rje mchog/ yang dang yang du gsor byed pa/
3b2(rgyud): khro gnyer rim pa ldan la sogs// lag na rdo rje mtha' yas po// dpo' bo
3b3(rgyud): gdul dka' 'dul ba po// 'jigs su rung dang dpa' bad can// rdo rje
3b4(rgyud): rtse mo rab 'phro ba// rang gi lag gi gsor byed pa// snying rje che dang shes
4a1(rgyud): / rab dang // thabs kyis 'gro don byed pa'i mchog
4a2(rgyud): dga' mgu rangs pa'i bsams pa can// khro bo lus kyi gzugs ldan pa/
4a3(rgyud): sangs rgyas 'phrin las byed pa'i mgon// lus btud rnams dang lhan
4a4(rgyud): cig du// mgon po bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs// rdzogs sangs
4b1(rgyud): rgyas la phyag 'tshal nas// thal mo sbyar bar byas nas ni// spyan sngar 'dug ste 'di skad gsol// khyab bdag
4b2(rgyud): bdag la sman pa dang // bdag don bdag la thugs brtse'i phyir// sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon rdzogs pa'i// byang
4b3(rgyud): chub ci nas bdag thob mdzod// nyon mongs pas ni sems dkrugs shing // mi shes 'dam du byin pa yi// sems
4b4(rgyud): can kun la sman pa dang // bla med 'bras bu thob bya'i phyir// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das// 'gro
4b5(rgyud): ba'i ma ston pa po// dam tshig chen po de nyid mkhyen// dbang po bsam pa mkhyen mchog gis// bcom
5a1(rgyud): ldan 'das kyis ye shes sku// gtsug gtor chen po tshig gi bdag/ ye shes sku
5a2(rgyud): ste rang byung ba// 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i ye// ming ni yang dag mchog/ don zab don ni rgya che zhing
5a3(rgyud): don chen mtshungs med rab zhi ba// thog ma par dang mthar dge ba// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis
5a4(rgyud): gsungs// ma 'ongs rnams kyang gsung 'gyur la// da ltar byung ba rdzogs sangs rgyas// yang dang yang du
5a5(rgyud): gsung ba gang // rgyud chen sgyu 'phrul dra ba las// rdo rje 'chang chen gsang sngags 'chang // dpag med
5b1(rgyud): rnams kyi dka' bzhin du// glur blangs gang lags bshad du gsol// mgon po rdzogs sangs rgyas kun gyi// gsang 'dzin ci
5b2(rgyud): nas bdag 'gyur phyir// nges par 'byung gi bar du 'di// bdag gi bsam pa brtan pos bzung // nyon mongs ma lus bsal ba dang /
5b3(rgyud): mi shes ma lus spang ba'i phyir// bsam pa'i khyad par ji bzhin du// sems can rnams la bshad par 'tshal// gsang dbang lag na rdo rje
5b4(rgyud): yis// de bzhin gshegs la de skad du// gsol nas thal mo sbyar byas te// lus btud nas ni spyan sngar 'dug/ zhus pa'i le'u ste
5b5(rgyud): dang po'o// / de nas bcom ldan shAkya thub// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rkang gnyis mchog/ nyid kyi zhal nas ljags bzang
5b6(rgyud): ba/ ring zhing yangs pa brkyang mdzad de// 'jig rten gsum po snang byed cing // bdud bzhi'i dgra rnams 'dul byed pa// sems can
6a1(rgyud): rnams kyi ngan song gsum// spong bar byed pa'i 'dzum bstan nas// tshangs pa'i gsungs ni snyen pa yis//
6a2(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum po kun bkang nas// lag na rdo rje stobs po che// gsang dbang la ni bslar gsungs pa// snying rje che dang ldan gyur pas// 'gro
6a3(rgyud): la phan pa'i don du khyod// ye shes lus can 'jam dpal gyi// ming brjod pas ni don che ba// dag par byed cing sdig sel ba// nga las nyan
6a4(rgyud): par brtson pa ni// legs so dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang // lag na rdo rje khyod legs so// gsang ba'i bdag de phyir ngas// khyod la legs par
6a5(rgyud): bstan par bya// khyod ni rtse gcig yid kyis nyon// bcom ldan de ni legs zhes gsol// lan slar gsungs pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o//
6a6(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan shakya thub// gsang sngags rigs chen thams cad dang // gsang sngags rigs sngags 'chang ba'i rigs// rigs
6b1(rgyud): gsum la ni rnam par gzigs// 'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa'i rigs// 'jig rten snang byed rigs chen dang // phyag rgya chen po'i rigs mchog dang /
6b2(rgyud): rin chen gtsug gtor cher gzigs nas// rigs drugs la gzigs pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// / tshigs gi bdag po tshigs su bcad/
6b3(rgyud): gsang sngags rgyal po drug ldan zhing // gnyis su med par 'byung ba dang // mi skye chos can 'di gsung ba// / a A/ i I/ u u/ e ai/ oM
6b4(rgyud): AM/ aM A/ s+thi to hri ti/ dz+nyA na pur ti ra haM bud to// bud d+ha naM/ tAd ta ba ra ti naM/ IM badz+ra tig Sh+Ta/ du kha tshe da/ prad dz+nyA dz+nyA na mur ta yai/ dz+nyA na ka ya/
6b5(rgyud): ba gi shwa ra/ a ra pa tsa na ya te ne ma// // sgyu 'phrul dra ba mngon par byang chub pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom
6b6(rgyud): ldan 'das// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas a las byung // a ni yig 'bru kun gyi mchog/ don chen yi ge dam pa yin// khong nas byung ba skye ba med// tshig
7a1(rgyud): rubya/ tu brjod pa spangs pa ste// brjod pa kun gyi rgyu yi mchog/ tshig kun rab tu gsal bar byed// mchod pa chen po 'dod chags
7a2(rgyud): pa che// sems can thams cad dga' bar byed// mchod pa chen po zhe sdang che// nyon mongs kun gyi dgra che ba// mchod pa chen po gti mug che// gti mug blo ste
7a3(rgyud): gti mug sel// mchod pa chen po khro ba che// khro ba chen po dgra che ba// mchod pa chen po chags pa che// chags pa thams cad sel bar byed// 'dod pa chen po
7a4(rgyud): bde ba che// dga' ba chen po mgu ba che// gzugs che lus kyang che ba ste// kha dog che zhing lus bongs che// ming yang che zhing rgya che ba// dkyil 'khor chen
7a5(rgyud): po yangs pa yin// shes rab mtshon chen 'chang ba ste// nyon mongs chen po lcags kyu mchog/ grags chen snyan grags chen po ste// snang ba chen po gsal
7a6(rgyud): ba che// mkhas pa sgyu 'phrul chen po 'chang // sgyu 'phrul chen po'i don grub pa// sgyu 'phrul chen po'i dga' bas dga'// sgyu 'phrul chen po mig 'phrul
7a7(rgyud): can sbyin bdag chen po gtso bo ste// tshul khrims chen po 'chang ba'i mchog/ bzod chen 'chang ba bsten pa po// brtson 'grus chen po brtul ba yin/
7b1(rgyud): bsam gtan chen po'i ting 'dzin gnas// shes rab chen po'i lus 'chang ba// stobs po che la thabs che ba// smon lam ye shes rgya mtsho ste// byams chen rang bzhin
7b2(rgyud): dpag tu med// snying rje chen po blo'i mchog/ shes rab chen po blo chen ldan// mkhas pa chen po thabs che ba// rdzu 'phrul chen po stobs dang ldan// shugs chen
7b3(rgyud): 'gyogs pa chen po ste// rdzu 'phrul chen po cher grags pa// stobs chen pha rol gnon pa po// srid pa'i ri bo chen po 'joms// mkhregs shing rdo rje chen po 'chang /
7b4(rgyud): drag po chen po drag shul che// 'jigs chen 'jigs par byed pa po// mgon po rigs mchog chen po ste// bla ma gsang sngags che ba'i mchog/ theg pa chen po'i tshul
7b5(rgyud): la gnas// theg pa chen po'i tshul gyi mchog/ byang sems rdo rje'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// / sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad che// thub pa chen po thub
7b6(rgyud): chen ldan// gsang sngags tshul chen las byung ba// gsang sngags tshul chen bdag nyid can// pha rol byin bcu thob pa ste// pha rol phyin bcu la gnas// pha rol
7b7(rgyud): byin bcu dag pa ste/ pha rol phyin pa bcu'i tshul// mgon pos bcu'i dbang phyug ste// sa bcu la ni gnas pa po// shes bcu rnam dge bdag nyid can// shes brgya
8a1(rgyud): rnam dag 'chang ba po// rnam pa bcu po don bcu'i don// thu dbang stobs bcu khyab pa'i bdag/ kun gyi don ni ma lus byed// rnam
8a2(rgyud): bcu dbang ldan che ba po// thog ma med pa spros med bdag/ de bzhin nyid bdag dag pa'i bdag/ bden par smra zhing tshig mi 'gyur// de skad smra ba de bzhin byed// gnyis
8a3(rgyud): su med dang gnyis med ston// yang dag mtha' las rnam par gnas// bdag med seng ge'i sgra dang ldan// mu stegs ri dgas ngan 'jigs byed/ kun tu 'gro ba'i don yod
8a4(rgyud): stobs// de bzhin gshegs pa'i yid ltar mgyog/ rgyal ba dgra rgyal rnam par rgyal// 'khor lo bsgyur ba stobs po che// tshogs kyi slob dpon tshogs kyi mchog/
8a5(rgyud): tshogs rje tshogs bdag dbang dang ldan// mthu chen bcas par 'dzin pa ste// tshul chen gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog/ tshig rje tshig bdag smras mkhas pa// tshig la dbang ba tshig
8a6(rgyud): mtha' yas// tshig bden pa dang bden par sla// bden pa bzhi ni ston pa po// phyir mi ldog pa phyir mi 'ong // 'dren pa rang rgyal bse ru'i tshul// nges 'byung sna
8a7(rgyud): tshogs las 'byung ba// 'byung ba chen po rgyu gcig po// dge slong dgra bcom zag pa zad // 'dod chags bral bas dbang po thul// bde ba rnyed pas 'jigs med cem
8b1(rgyud): bsil bar gyur pas rnyog pa med// rig pa dang ni rkang par ldan// bde gshegs 'jig rten rig pa'i mchog/ bdag gir mi 'dzin ngar mi 'dzin// bden pa gnyis kyi/
8b2(rgyud): tshul gnas// 'khor ba'i pha rol mthar son pa// bya ba byas pa skam sar gnas// shes pa 'be' zhig nges bsal ba// shes rab mtshon chas rnams 'joms pa//
8b3(rgyud): dam chos chos rgyal gsal bar ldan// 'jig rten snang bar byed pa'i mchog/ chos kyi dbang phyug chos kyi rgyal// legs pa'i lam ni ston pa po// don grub bsam pa
8b4(rgyud): grub pa ste// kun tu rtog pa thams cad spangs// rnam par mi rtog dbyings mi zad// chos dbyings dam pa zad mi shes// bsod nams ldan pa bsod nams tshogs/
8b5(rgyud): ye shes ye shes 'byung gnas che// ye shes ldan pa yod med shes// tshogs gnyis tshogs ni bsags pa po// rtag pa kun rgyal rnal 'byor can// bsam gtan bsam
8b6(rgyud): bya blo ldan mchog/ so sor rang rig mi g.yo ba// mchog dbang po sku gsum 'chang // sangs rgyas lnga'i bdag nyid can// khyab bdag ye shes lnga'i bdag/ sangs
8b7(rgyud): rgyas lnga bdag cod pan can// spyan lnga chags pa med pa 'chang // sa kyis ma ya ma / mam mig/ shes pa srid 'byung skye gnas med// chos las 'byung ba
9a1(rgyud): srid pa sel// gcig pu sra 'khregs rdo rje'i bdag/ skyes ma thag tu 'gro ba'i bdag/ nam mkha' las 'byung rang 'byung ba// shes
9a2(rgyud): rab ye shes me bo che// 'od chen rnam par snang bar byed// ye shes snang ba lam me ba// 'gro ba'i mar me ye shes sgron// gzi brjid phung po 'od bsal ba// sngags chog
9a3(rgyud): mnga' bdag rigs sngags rgyal// gsang sngags rgyal po don chen byed// gtsug tor chen po rmad 'byung gtsug/ nam mkha'i bdag po sna tshogs ston// sangs rgyas kun
9a4(rgyud): bdag dngos po mchog/ 'gro kun dga' ba'i mig dang ldan// sna tshogs gzugs can bskyed pa po// mchod cing brjod pa drang srong che// rigs gsum 'chang ba gsang
9a5(rgyud): sngags 'chang // dam tshig chen po gsang sngags 'dzin// gtso bo dkon mchog gsum 'dzin pa// theg pa mchog gsum ston pa po// don yod zhags pa rnam par rgyal/
9a6(rgyud): 'dzin pa chen po rdo rje zhabs// rdo rje lcags kyu zhags pa che// chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes la bstod pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// rdo rje 'jigs byed 'jigs par byed/
9a7(rgyud): khro bo'i rgyal po gdong drug 'jigs// mig drug lag drug stobs dang ldan// keng rus mche ba brtsigs pa po// ha la ha la gdong brgya pa// gshin rje gshed pa
9b1(rgyud): bgegs kyi rgyal// rdo rje shugs chen 'jigs byed// rdo rje grags pa rdo rje snying // sgyu 'phrul rdo rje gsus po che// rdo rje las skyes rdo rje'i bdag/ rdo rje snying po mkha'
9b2(rgyud): 'dra ba// mi g.yo ral pa gcig gis bgyings// glang chen ko rlon gos su gyon// grag chen ha ha zhes sgrogs pa// hi hi zhes sgrogs 'jigs par byed// gad mo chen po
9b3(rgyud): gad rgyangs can// rdo rje gad mo cher sgrogs pa// rdo rje sems dpa' sems dpa' che// rdo rje rgyal po bde ba che// rdo rje drag po dga' ba che// rdo rje hUM ste hUM zhes sgrogs/
9b4(rgyud): mtshon du rdo rje mda' thogs pa// rdo rje ral gris ma lus gcod// rdo rje kun 'chang rdo rje can// rdo rje gcig pu g.yul sel ba// rdo rje 'bar ba mig mi zad // sku
9b5(rgyud): yang rdo rje 'bar ba ste// rdo rje 'bebs pa 'bebs pa che// mig brgya pa ste rdo rje'i mig/ lus ni rdo rje ba spu can// rdo rje'i spu ni gcig spu'i lus// sen mo skyes pa
9b6(rgyud): rdo rje'i rtse// rdo rje snying po lpags pa mkhregs// rdo rje'i phreng thogs dpal dang ldan// rdo rje'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa ste// gad rgyangs ha ha nges par sgrogs// yi ge drug
9b7(rgyud): pardo rje'i sgra// 'jam dbyangs chen po dgra che ba// 'jig rten gsum na sgra gcig pa// na mkha'i khams las sgra sgrogs pa// sgra dang ldan pa rnams kyi mchog
10a1(rgyud): me long lta bu'i ye shes la bstod pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // yang dag bdag med de bzhin nyid// yang dag mtha'
10a2(rgyud): ste yi ge med// stong nyid smra ba'i khyung mchog ste// zab cing rgya che'i sgra sgrogs pa// chos kyi dung ste sgra chen ldan// chos kyi g+han de sgra bo che// mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa po//
10a3(rgyud): phyogs bcu chos kyi rnga bo che// gzugs med gzugs bzang dam pa ste// sna tshogs gzugs can yid las skyes// gzugs rnams thams cad snang ba'i dpal/
10a4(rgyud): gzugs brnyan ma lus 'chang ba po// tshugs pa med cing che bar grags// khams gsum dbang phyug chen po ste// 'phags lam shin du mtho la gnas// dar ba chen po/
10a5(rgyud): chos kyi tog/ 'jig rten gsum na gzhon lus gcig/ gnas brten rgan po skye dgu'i bdag/ sum bcu rtsa gnyis mtshan 'chang ba// sdug gu 'jig rten gsum na
10a6(rgyud): mangs// 'jig rten shas lags slob dpon ste/ 'jig ten slob dpon 'jigs pa med// mgon slobs 'jig rten ming gtsug pa// srubs dang stobs pa dran
10a7(rgyud): med// namakha'i mtha' la longs spyod pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mtsho// ma rig sgo nga'i srubs 'byed pa// srid pa'i dra ba 'joms pa po// nyon mongs
10b1(rgyud): ma lus zhi byed pa// 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho pha rol byin// ye shes dbang skur cod pan can// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rgyan du thogs// sdug bsngal gsum gyi sdug
10b2(rgyud): bsngal zhi// gsum sel mtha' yas grol gsum thob// sgrib pa kun las nges par grol// mkha' ltar mnyam pa nyid la gnas// nyon mongs dri ma kun las 'das//
10b3(rgyud): dus gsum dus med rtogs pa po// sems can kun gyi glu chen po// yon tan thod can rnams kyi thod// nyon mongs kun las rnam par grol// na mkha'i lam la rab
10b4(rgyud): gnas pa// yid bzhin nor bu chen po 'chang // khyab bdag rin chen kun gyi mchog/ dpag bsam shing chen rgyas pa ste// bum pa bzang po che ba'i mchog/ byed pa
10b5(rgyud): sems can kun don byed// phan 'dogs sems can gnyis gshin pa// bzang ngan shes shing dus shes pa// khyab bdag dam shes dam tshig ldan// dus shes sems
10b6(rgyud): can dbang po shes// rnam grol gsum la mkhas pa po// yon tan ldan zhing yon tan shes// chos shes bkra shis bkra shis 'byung // bkra shis kun gyi bkra shis
10b7(rgyud): pa grags pa'i bkra shis sman grags dge// dbugs 'byin chen po dga' ston che// dga' chen rol mo chen po ste// bkur sti rim gro phun sum tshogs
11a1(rgyud): @mchog du dga' ba'i grags dag dpal// mchog ldan mchog sbyin gtso bo ste// skangs kyi dam pa srubs su 'os// 'jigs chen dgra/
11a2(rgyud): rab kyi mchog/ 'jigs pa ma lus sel ba bo// tsug pud dpung bu lcang lo can// ral pa mun dza cod pan thogs// gdong lnga gtsug pungad lnga dang ldan// zur phung lnga pa
11a3(rgyud): me tog thod// mgo zlum brtul shugs chen po pa// tshangs par spyod pa rtul zhugs mchog/ dka' thub mthar byin dka' thub che// gtsang gnas dam pa go'u tam/
11a4(rgyud): bram ze tshangs pa tshangs pa che// mya ngan 'das pa tshangs pas thob// grol ba thar pa rnam grol lus// rnam grol zhi ba zhi ba nyid// mya ngan 'das ni mya ngan 'das/
11a5(rgyud): legs par mya ngan 'das dang nye// bde sdug sel ba mthar gyur pa// chags bral lus las 'das pa po// thub pa med pa dpe med pa// mi mngon mi snang bsal byed min
11a6(rgyud): mi 'gyur kun 'gro khyab pa po// phra zhing zag med sa bon bral// rdul med rdul bral dri ma med// nyes pa spangs pa skyon med pa// shin du sad pa sad pa'i bdag/ kun
11a7(rgyud): shes kun rigs dam pa po// rnam par shes pa'i chos nyid 'das// ye shes gnyis med tshul 'chang ba// rnam par rtog med lhun gyi grub// dus gsum sangs rgyas
11b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas thog ma tha ma med// dang po'i sangs rgyas rgyu med pa// dge migs sa rjo na// le shes su na seMn gshes/ tshig gi dbang phyug smra ba che// smra ba'i skyes mchog smra ba'i
11b2(rgyud): rgyal/ smra ba'i dam pa mchog gi gnas// smra ba'i seng ge tshugs pa med// kun tu lta ba mchog tu dga'// gzi brjid phreng ba blta na sdug/ 'od bzang 'bar
11b3(rgyud): ba dpal gyi be'u// lag na 'od 'bar snang ba po// sman pa che mchog gtso bo ste// zung rngu 'byin pa bla na med// sman rnams ma lus ljon pa'i shing // nad do cog
11b4(rgyud): gi dgra che ba// sdug gu 'jig rten gsum gyi mchog/ dpal ldan rgyu skar dkyil 'khor can// phyogs bcu nam mkha'i mthar thug par// chos kyi rgyal mtshan
11b5(rgyud): legs par 'dzugs// 'gro na gdugs gcig yangs pa ste// byams dang snying rje'i dkyil 'khor can// dpal ldan pad ma gar gyi bdag/ khyab bdag
11b6(rgyud): chen po rin chen gdugs// sangs rgyas kun gyi gzi brjid che// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku 'chang ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi rnal 'byor che// sangs rgyas kun gyi bstan pa
11b7(rgyud): gcig/ rdo rje rin chen dbang skur dpal// rin chen kun bdag dbang phyug ste// 'jig rten dbang phyug kun gyi bdag/ rdo rje 'chang ba kun gyi rje// sangs rgyas
12a1(rgyud): kun gyi thugs che ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs la gnas// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku che ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung yang yin/
12a2(rgyud): rje nyi ma snang ba che// rdo rje zla ba dri med 'od// chags bral la sogs chags pa che// kha dog sna tshogs 'bar ba'i 'od// rdo rje dkyil dkrung rdzogs sangs rgyas// sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i
12a3(rgyud): chos 'dzin pa// dpal ldan sangs rgyas pad ma skyes// kun mkhyen ye shes mdzod 'dzin pa// rgyal po sgyu 'phrul sna tshogs 'chang // che ba sangs rgyas rigs sngags rgyal/
12a4(rgyud): rdo rje rnon po ral gri che// yi ge mchog ste rnam par dag/ theg pa chen pos sdug bsngal gcod// mtshon chen po rdo rje chos// rdo rje zab mo 'dzin na 'jig/ rdo rje blo gros don
12a5(rgyud): bzhin rigs// pha rol phyin pa kun rdzogs pa// sa rnams kun gyi rgyan dang ldan// rnam par dag pa bdag med chos// yang dag ye shes zla 'od bzang // brtson chen sgyu
12a6(rgyud): 'phrul dra ba la// rgyud kun gyi ni bdag po mchog/ rdo rje gdan ni ma lus ldan// ye shes sku rnams ma lus 'chang // kun tu bzang po blo gros bzang // sa yi snying po 'gro
12a7(rgyud): ba 'dzin// sangs rgyas kun gyi snying po che// sprul pa'i 'khor lo sna tshogs 'chang // dngos po kun gyi rang bzhin mchog/ dngos po kun gyi rang bzhin 'dzin// soso pa
12b1(rgyud): rtogs pa'i legs la stod pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// / skye med chos te sna tshogs don// chos kun ngo bo nyid 'chang ba// shes rab chen po skad
12b2(rgyud): cig la// chos kun khong du chud pa 'chang // chos kun mngon par rtogs pa ste// thub pa blo mchog 'byung po'i mtha'// mi g.yo rab tu dang ba'i bdag/ rdzogs pa'i sangs
12b3(rgyud): rgyas byang chub 'chang // sangs rgyas kun gyi mngon gsum pa// ye shes me lce 'od rab gsal// 'dod pa'i don grub dam pa ste// ngan song thams cad rnam sbyong ba/
12b4(rgyud): mgon po sems can kun gyi mchog/ sems can thams cad rab grol byed// nyon mongs g.yul du gcig dpa' ba// mi shes dgra yi dregs pa 'joms// blo ldan sgeg
12b5(rgyud): 'chang dpal dang ldan// brtan po mi sdug gzugs 'chang ba// lag pa brgya po kun skyod cing // gom pa'i stabs kyi gar byed pa// dpal ldan lag pa brgyas gang la/
12b6(rgyud): nam mkha' khyab par gar byed pa/ sa yi dkyil 'khor bzhi'i khyon// rkang pa ya gcig mthil gyis gnon// rkang 'theb sen me'i khyon gyis kyang // tshangs pa'i yu
12b7(rgyud): sa rtse nas gnon// don gcig gnyis med chos kyi don// dam pa'i don te 'jigs pa med// rnam rig sa tshogs gzugs don can// sems dang rnam shes rgyud dang ldan
13a1(rgyud): dngos don ma lus rnams la dga'// stong pa nyid dga' 'dod chags blo// srid pa'i 'dod chags sogs spangs pa// srid gsum
13a2(rgyud): dga' ba chen po pa// sprin dkar dag pa bzhin du dkar// 'od bzangs ston ka'i zla ba'i 'od// nyi ma'i char ka'i dkyil ltar mdzes// sen mo'i 'od ni shas cher dmar/
13a3(rgyud): cod pan bzang po mthon ka'i rtse// skra mchog 'thon ka chen po can// nor bu chen po 'od chags dpal// sangs rgyas sprul pa'i rgyan dang ldan// 'jig rten khams brgya
13a4(rgyud): kun spyod cing // rdzu 'phrul rkang pa'i stobs dang ldan// de nyid dran pa chen po 'chang// dran pa bzhi pa'i ting 'dzin rgyal// byang chub yan lag me tog spos// de bzhin
13a5(rgyud): gshegs pa'i yon tan mtsho// lam gyi yan lag brgyad tshul rigs// yang dag sangs rgyas lam rig pa// sems can kun la shas cher chags// nam mkha'
13a6(rgyud): lta bur chags pa med// sems can gyi yid la 'jug/ sems can kun gyi yid ltar 'gyog// sems can kun gyi dbang don shes// sems can kun gyis yid 'phrog
13a7(rgyud): ba/ phung po lnga don de nyid shes// rnam dag phung po lnga 'chang ba// nges 'byung kun gyi mtha' la gnas// nges par 'byung ba kun la mkhas// nges 'byung kun gyi/
13b1(rgyud): le gnas// nges par 'byung ba kun ston pa// yan lag bcu gnyis srid rtsa bton// dag pa rnam pa bcu gnyis 'chang // bden bzhi'i tshul gyi rnam pa can// shes pa
13b2(rgyud): brgyad po rtogs pa 'chang // bden don rnam pa bcu gnyis ldan// de nyid rnam pa bcu drug rig/ rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa// rnam par sangs rgyas kun rig mchog/
13b3(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi sprul pa'i// bye ba dpag med 'gyed pa po// skad cig thams cad mngon par rtogs// sems kyi skad cig don kun rig/ theg pa sna tshogs thabs
13b4(rgyud): tshul gyis// 'gro ba'i don la rtogs pa po// theg pa gsum gyi nges 'byung la// theg pa gcig gi 'bras bur gnas// nyon mongs khams rnams dag pa'i bdag/ las
13b5(rgyud): kyi khams rnams zad byed pa// chu bo'i rgya mtsho kun las rgal// sbyor ba'i dgon pa las byung ba// nyon mongs nye ba kun nyon mongs// bag chags bcas pa gtan spangs
13b6(rgyud): pa/ snying rje chen po shes rab thabs// don yod 'gro ba'i don byed pa/ 2/ 'du shes kun gyi don spangs shing // rnams shes don ni 'gag par byed// sems ca
13b7(rgyud): kun yid yul dang ldan// sems can kun gyi yid rig pa// sems can kun gyi yid la gnas// de dag sems dang 'thun par 'jug/ sems can kun yid tshim par byed/
14a1(rgyud): @#sems can kun gyi yid dga' ba// grub pa mthar phyin 'khrul pa med// nor pa thams cad rnam par spangs// don gsum thotsom med pa'i
14a2(rgyud): blo/ kun don yon tan gsum gyi bdag/ phung po lnga don dus gsum du// skad cig thams cad bye brag phyed// skad cig gcig gis rdzogs sangs rgyas// sangs rgyas
14a3(rgyud): kun gyi rang bzhin 'chang // lus med lus ste lus kyi mchog/ lus kyi mtha' ni rtogs pa po// gzugs rnams sna tshogs kun du ston// nor bu chen po rin chen tog/
14a4(rgyud): mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi le'u ste dgu pa'o// // sangs rgyas kun gyi rtogs bya ba// sangs rgyas byang chub bla na med// gsang sngags las byung yi ge
14a5(rgyud): med// gsang sngags chen po rigs gsum pa// gsang snga gdon kun skyed pa po// thig le chen po yi ge med// stong pa chen po yi ge med// thig le stong pa yi ge
14a6(rgyud): brgya/ rnam pa kun ldan rnam pa med// bcu drug phyed phyed thig le can// yan lag med pa'i rtsis las 'das// bsam gtan bzhi pa'i rtse mo can// bsam
14a7(rgyud): gtan yan lag kun shes shing // ting 'dzin rig dang rgyud rig pa// ting 'dzin lus can lus kyi mchog/ longs spyod rdzogs sku kun las rgyal// sprul pa'i ste sku
14b1(rgyud): sku'i mchog/ sangs rgyas sprul pa'i rgyud 'chang ba// phyogs bcur sprul pa sna tshogs 'gyed// ji bzhin 'gro ba'i don byed pa// lha dang lnga dbang lha yi lha// lha'i
14b2(rgyud): bdag po lha min bdag/ 'chi med dbang po lha'i bla// 'joms byed 'joms dbang phyug po// srid pa'i dgon pa las rgal ba// ston pa gcig pu 'gro ba'i bla// 'jig
14b3(rgyud): rten phyogs bcur rab grags pa// chos kyi sbyin bdag che ba po// byams pa'i go cha chas pa ste// snying rje yi ni yan lag bgos// shes rab ral gri mnga' gzhu thog/
14b4(rgyud): nyon mongs mi shes g.yul ngo sel// dpa' bo bdud dgra bdud 'dul// bdud bzhi'i 'jigs pa sel bar byed// bdud kyi dpungs rnams pa ma byed pa// rdzogs pa'i
14b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas 'jig rten 'dren// mchod 'os stod 'os phyag gi gnas// rtag tu rim gro bya ba'i 'os// bkur 'os brjed par bya ba'i mchog/ phyag byar 'os pa bla ma'i
14b6(rgyud): rab// 'jig rten gsum po gom gcig bgrod// mkha' ltar mtha' med rnam par gnon// gsum rig gtsang ma dag pa ste// mngon shes drug ldan rdzas dran drug/
14b7(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che// rdzu 'phrul chen po 'jig rten 'das// shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i mtha'// shes rab kyis ni de nyid thob// bdag rigs gzhan
15a1(rgyud): rig thams cad la// kun la phan pa'i gang zag mchog/ dper bya kun las 'das pa ste// shes dang shes bya'i bdag po mchog/ gtso ga
15a2(rgyud): chos kyi sbyin ste// phyag rgya bzhi po'i don ston pa// 'gro ba'i bsnyen bkur gnas kyi mchog/ nges 'byung gsum po bgrod rnams kyi// don gyi dam pa rnam dag dpal//
15a3(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum na bskal bzang che// dpal ldan 'byor pa kun byed pa// 'jam dpal dpal dang ldan pa'i mchog/ bya ba grub pa'i ye shes la bstod pa'i le'u ste/
15a4(rgyud): bcu pa'o// / bcod sbyin rdo rje mchog khyod 'dud// yang dag mthar gyur khyod la 'dud// stod nyid las byung khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas byang chub
15a5(rgyud): khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas chags pa khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas 'dod la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sangs rgyas dgos pa khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas rol la phyan/
15a6(rgyud): 'tshal 'dud// sangs rgyas 'dzum pa khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas bzhad la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sangs rgyas gsung nyid khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas thugs
15a7(rgyud): la phyag 'tshal 'dud// med pa las byung khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas 'byung ba khyod la 'dud// nam mkha' las byung khyod la 'dud// ye shes byung khye
15b1(rgyud): la 'dud// sgyu 'phrul dra ba khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas rol ston khyod la 'dud// thams cad thams cad khyod la 'dud// ye shes sku nyid khyod la 'dud// ye shes/
15b2(rgyud): lnga'i sgo nas rigs lnga la bstod pa'i le'u ste bcug pa'o// / lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chang // 'di ni bcom ldan 'das kyi ye shes sku// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
15b3(rgyud): cad kyi ye shes kyi sku// 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i yongs su dag pa thun mong ma yin pa'i ming yang dag brjod pa yin te// khyod kyi dga' ba dang / dad pa dang /
15b4(rgyud): mgu ba chen po bla na med pa bskyed pa dang // lus dang ngag dang yid kyi gsang ba yongs su dag par bya ba dang / yongs su ma rdzogs pa dang // yongs su dag pa'i pha rol tu phyin
15b5(rgyud): pa dang // bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rnams yongs su rdzogs shing // yongs su dag par bya ba dang // bla na med pa'i don ma rtogs pa rtogs par bya ba dang /
15b6(rgyud): ma thob pa thob par bya ba nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam pa'i chos kyi tshul yang dag par bzung ba'i phyir// ngas bshad cing bstan te dgrol zhing rnam
15b7(rgyud): par phye la gsal bar byas so// byin gyis brlab par bya'o// nga/ lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chang / 'di ni ngas khyod kyi rgyud la yang gsang sngags thams cad kyi chos nyid
16a1(rgyud): @byin gyis brlabs kyis byin gyis brlabs so// lag na rdo rje 'chang // gzhan yang ming yang dag par brjod pa 'di ni de
16a2(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shin du yongs su dag cing yongs su byang ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang bar gyur pa'o//
16a3(rgyud): shin du yongs su dag cing shin tu yongs su byang ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi byang chub po/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
16a4(rgyud): rnams kyi mngon par rtogs pa'o// bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyi// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings bla na med pa thugs su chud pa'o// /
16a5(rgyud): rgyal ba rnams kyi bdud kyi stobs thams cad pham par mdzad pa'o// stobs bcu dang ldan pa rnams kyi stobs bcu'i stobs nyid do// thams cad mkhyen pa rnam
16a6(rgyud): kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi lung ngo // sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag par bsgrubs pa'o// byang chub sems
16a7(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad kyi bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa dri ma med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// nyan thos dang rang
16b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi skye gnas so// lha dang mi thams cad phun sum tshogs pa thams cad kyi zhing ngo // theg pa chen po'i gzhi'o// byang chub sems dpa'i
16b2(rgyud): spyod pa rnams kyi 'byung khungs so// 'phags pa'i lam thams cad kyi mtha'o// rnam par grol ba rnams brtags pa'o// nges par 'byung ba'i lam skye ba'i
16b3(rgyud): gnas so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung mi 'chad pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i rigs dang rgyud rab tu 'phel ba'o// pararo rgol
16b4(rgyud): ba thams cad tshar gcod pa'o// mu stegs can thams cad rnam par 'joms pa'o// bdud bzhi'i stobs kyi dpung gi sde pham par byed pa'o// sems can
16b5(rgyud): thams cad yang dag par bsdud pa'o// nges par 'byung ba bgrod pa thams cad kyi 'phags pa'i lam yongs su smin pa'o// tshangs pa'i bzhi la gnas pa rnam
16b6(rgyud): kyi ting nge 'dzin to// sems rtse gcig pa rnams kyi bsam gtan no// lus dang ngag dang yid 'dul ba la brtson pa rnams kyi rnal 'byor ro// kun tu sbyor ba
16b7(rgyud): thams cad dang bral ba'o// gnyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spong ba'o// sgrib pa thams cad nye bar zhi ba'o// 'ching ba thams cad las rnam
17a1(rgyud): par grol ba'o// rdzas thams cad las thar pa'o// sems kyi g.yeng ba thams cad zhi ba'o// 'byor pa zad kyi 'byung gnas so// rgud pa thams cad kyi 'byung
17a2(rgyud): gnas so// rgud pa zad sel ba'o// ngan song gi sgo thams gcod pa'o// rnam par grol ba'i grong khyer gyi lam bzang po'o// 'khor ba'i 'khor lo la mi 'jug pa'o// chos kyi 'khor lo
17a3(rgyud): bskor ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stan pa'i gdugs dang // rgyal mtshan dang ba dan bsgreng ba'o// dam pa'i chos ston pa'i gnas so// byang chub sems dpa' gsang sngags kyi sgo'i/
17a4(rgyud): spyad pa spyod pa rnams kyi myur du grub pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mngon par brtson pa rnams kyi sgom pa rtogs pa'o// gnyis su med pa'i so sor rtog pa/
17a5(rgyud): bsgom pa la mngon par brtson pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid so sor rtog pa'o// gnyis su med par so sor rtogs par mngon par brtson pa rnams kyi rdzogs pa'o// pha rol du phyin pa dang tsho gas thad/
17a6(rgyud): nges par 'grub pa'o// sa thaMd yongs su rdzogs pa'o// 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po rnams yang dag par 'grub pa'o// chos thams cad kyi dran pa nye bar bzhag pa bzhi po rnams kyi
17a7(rgyud): sems rtse gcig so sor rtogs pa'o// mtshan yang dag par brjod pa 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thams cad kyi bar du yang yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'o// lag na rdo rdo rje 'chang /
17b1(rgyud): gzhan yang ming yang dag par brjod pa 'di ni sems can tha~Md kyi lus dang ngag dang yid las kun du spyod pa'i sdig pa ma lus pa rab du zhi bar byed pa'o// sems can thams cad kyi ngan song tha
17b2(rgyud): rnam par sbyong ba'o// ngan 'gro thams cad bzlog pa'o// las kyi sgrib pa thams cad yang dag par bcod pa'o// mi khom pa thams cad kyi skye ba'i rgyun mi skye bar byed pa'o// 'jig pa chen
17b3(rgyud): po brgyad zhi bar byed pa'o// rmi lam ngan pa thaMd nges par 'jig par byed pa'o// ltas ngan pa thams cad nges par sel ba'o// brda' ngas dang dgra bgegs thams cad rnam par zhi bar byed pa'o//
17b4(rgyud): bdud kyi dgra'i las tha~Md ring du spong bar byed pa'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba dang bsod nams thams cad 'phel bar byed pa'o// tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i yid la byed pa thaMd mi skye bar byed pa'o// /
17b5(rgyud): rgyag pa dang nga rgyal dang dreg pa dang ngar 'dzin pa ma lus par 'joms par byed pa'o// sdug bsngal ba dang // yid mi bde ba thams cad mi skye bar byed pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thaMd kyi snyi/
17b6(rgyud): por 'gyur ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' tha~Md kyi gsang bar 'gyur ba'o// nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang chen du gyur pa'o// phyag rgya dang gsang sngags thaMd du gyur pa'o// chos
17b7(rgyud): zad brjod du med par smra ba rnas kyi dran pa dang shes bzhin yang dag par bskyed pa'o// bla na med pa'i shes rab bskyed pa dang / yid gzhungs par byed pa'o// nad med pa dang /
18a1(rgyud): bya/ stobs dang dbang phyug phun sum tshogs par byed pa'o// dpal dang dge ba dang zhi ba dang legs pa rab tu 'phel bar byed pa'i/
18a2(rgyud): grags pa dang snyan pa dang / tshigs su bcad pa dang / bstod pa dang grags par byed pa'o// nad dang 'jigs pa chen po thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa'o//
18a3(rgyud): shin tu dag pa rnams kyi yang shin tu dag pa'o// shin tu dag byed rnams kyi yang shin du dag byed do// rab tu byung ba rnams kyi yang rab tu byang ba'o// rab tu bkra shis pa
18a4(rgyud): rnams kyi yang rab tu bkra shis pa'o// skyabs 'dod pa nas kyi yang skyabs so// gnas med pa rnams kyi yang gnas so// skyob po 'dod pa rnams kyi yang skyob pa'o//
18a5(rgyud): dpung snyan 'dod pa rnams kyi yang dpung gnyen no// gling 'dod pa rnams kyi gling ngo // 'a khra sa 'dod pa rnams kyi khra sa bla na med pa'o// srid pa'i rgya mtsho'i pha rol du
18a6(rgyud): 'gro ba rnams kyi gru'o// nad thams cad sel bar byed pa'i sman gyi rgyal po'o// blang bya dang dor bya'i dngos po bye brag phyed pa'i shes rab nyid do// lta ba ngan pa'i
18a7(rgyud): mun nag thams cad yang dag par sel bar byed pa'i ye shes kyi snang ba'o// sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su rdzogs
18b1(rgyud): par byed pa'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu'o// 'jam dpal ye shes kyi sku thob par bya ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes so// spyan lnga thob par bya ba'i
18b2(rgyud): ye shes mthong ba yongs su thob pa'o// zang zing dang mi 'jigs pa dang chos kyi sbyin pa gtong ba'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs pa'o// bsod nams
18b3(rgyud): dang ye shes kyi tsho gas dang ting nge 'dzin yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir sa bcu yongs su rdzogs pa'o// chos nyid dang bral ba'i phyir gnyis su med pa'i chos nyid do// sgro btags
18b4(rgyud): pa med pa'i phyir de bzhin nyid dang gzhan ma yin pa'i chos nyid do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i yongs su dag pa'i ngo bo nyid yin pa'i mtha'i rang bzhin nyid do// kalta ba ngan pa'i
18b5(rgyud): tshang tshing brgya stong ma lus pa sel ba'i phyir rnam pa thams cad rnam pa med pa stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin nyid do// mtshan yang dag par brjod pa 'di ni 'di lta ste// gnyis su
18b6(rgyud): med pa'i chos nyid kyi don gyi mtshan yang dag par 'dzin pa ston pa'i phyir chos thams cad brjod du med pa'i rang bzhin nyid do// lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chang // gzhan yang rigs
18b7(rgyud): kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gsang sngags kyi sgo'i spyad pa spyod pa gang la la/ bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal ya nas sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thams
19a1(rgyud): cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes su// gnyis su med pa'i don dam pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pa mtshan gyi gtsug gi nor bu 'di thams/
19a2(rgyud): cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang // ma nyams shing lhag chad med par tshigs su bcad pa'i tshig dang // yig 'bru 'di dag nyid kyis nyin gcig bzhin du dus gsum du 'chang ba
19a3(rgyud): dang / klog pa dang kun chub par byed pa dang // tshul bzhin du yid la byed pa dang // gzhan dag la yang dam tshigs bzhin du ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / ming gi don
19a4(rgyud): gang yang rung ba re re nas kyang 'jam dpal ye shes sems pa'i sku dmigs te kun nas sgo'i gnas pas gnas pa dang // chos thams cad rtogs pa'i mchog rnyog pa med pa'i
19a5(rgyud): dad pa dang ldan bzhin pa dang // mos pa dang / de kho na nyid yid la byed pas/ sems rtse gcig tu sgom pa de la ni/ dus gsum gyi dus med pa dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas
19a6(rgyud): dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad 'dus te gshegs nas/ chos kyi sgo thams cad ston par mdzad de/ sku yang ston to// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' tham
19a7(rgyud): cad kyis byin gyis rlob par mdzad de/ sku dang gsung dang thugs thams cad kyis de'i rgyud la yang dag par byin gyis slob bo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'adzang/
19b1(rgyud): kyis phan gdags pas phan 'dogs par mdzad do// chos thams cad la mi 'jigs pa yang grub par mdzad do// dgra bcom pa dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad
19b2(rgyud): dang 'phag pa'i chos la sdug par 'dzin pa'i bsams pas bdag nyid kyi dngos po yang nye bar ston par mdzad do// ma rungs pa 'dul ba'i khro bo'i rgyal po rnams dang / rdo
19b3(rgyud): rje 'chang chen po la sogs pa 'gro ba yongs su skyob pa rnams sprul pa'i sku sna tshogs kyi mdangs dang / stobs dang gzi brjid zil gyis mi non pa dang / gsang sngags dang /
19b4(rgyud): phyag rgya dang / mngon par rtogs pa dang / dkyil 'khor thams cad sgrub par byed pa'o// gsang sngags dang rig sngags kyi rgyal mo ma lus pa dang // bgegs dang / los
19b5(rgyud): 'dren dang / bdud kyi dgra dang phyir bzlog pa dang / gzhan gyis mi thub pa thams cad kyang nyin mtshan phyed par skad cig re re la spyod lam thams du bsrung ba dang / skyob pa dang /
19b6(rgyud): sbed par byed do// tshangs pa dang / dbang po dang nye dbang po dang / drag po dang mtshan po che dang // kun 'gyed gzhon nu dang // dbang phyug chen po dang / smin drug gi bu dang /
19b7(rgyud): nag po chen po dang / dga' byed dbang phyug dang / gshin rje dang / chu lba dang / dku ber dang / 'phrog ma dang / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten skyong ba gang yin pa de dag kyang / dang

20b1(rgyud): yin pa rnams dang / gnod sbyin mo rnams dang / srin mo dang / sha za mo gang yin pa de dag thams cad kyang 'du zhing / gcig tu 'thun par yongs su rdzogs pa'i dpung dang
20b2(rgyud): bcas/ 'khor dang bcas pas bsrung ba dang / skyob pa dang / sbed pa thams cad byed par 'gyur ro// mdangs dang / stobs dang / gzi brjid mchog kyang de'i lus

20b5(rgyud): sems dpa'i gzugs yid la dmigs shing / gzugs 'thun par dmigs te/ de'i gzugs dang 'thun par bsam gtan byed pa ni/ 'dul ba'i dbang gis ring

20b7(rgyud): dang ldan pa/ na mkha'i dkyil na bzhugs pa mthong bar 'gyur ro// sems can chen po de ni rnams kyang ji ltar 'gyur kyang / ngan song du ltung bar mi 'gyur ro// rigs
21a1(rgyud): ngan du skye bar mi 'gyur ro// dbang po ma tshang bar mi 'gyur ro// log par lta ba dang / lta ba ngan pa'i rigs su skye bar mi 'gyur ro//

21a3(rgyud): tshe rings po'i rnams kyi nang du skye bar mi 'gyur ro// mu ge dang nad dang mtshon gyi skal pa'i nang du yang skye bar mi 'gyur ro// rgyal po dang dgra dang chom rkun gyi 'jigs pa
21a4(rgyud): yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// ji nas kyang dman pa dang / dbul ba'i 'jigs pa yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// dri ngas dang bskur ba dang / smad pa dang / mi gnyen pa
21a5(rgyud): dang / gtam ngan gyi 'jigs pa yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// rgyud dang rus dang rigs bzang po dang yang ldan par 'gyur ro// kun nas mdzes pa dang gzugs

21b1(rgyud): longs spyod kyi gzhi che ba dang / 'khor mang ba dang / longs spyod kyi gzhi mi zad pa dang / 'khor mi zad par yang 'gyur ro// sems can thams cad kyi mchog dang /

21b3(rgyud): sgrin por yang 'gyur ro// shes nyen can dang / le lo med pa dang / chog shes pa dang / nor mang ba dang / sred pa med par yang 'gyur ro// sems can thams cad kyi mchog
21b4(rgyud): tu yid brtan pa bya ba dang / slob dpon dang bla mar bkur bar yang 'gyur ro// des sngon ma thos pa'i bzo dang / rang bzhin gyis pha rol du phyin pa drug gi yon tan dang ldan par
21b5(rgyud): 'gyur ro// tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi la gnas par 'gyur ro// dran pa dang / shes bzhin dang thabs dang / stobs dang smon lam dang / ye shes dang yang ldan par 'gyur//
21b6(rgyud): sgyu rtsal dang mngon par shes pa'i shes pa dang / bstan bcos thams cad kyang don dang yi ge'i sgo nas shes par 'gyur ro// tshul khrims dang / 'tsho ba dang / kun tu spyod
21b7(rgyud): po shin tu yongs su dag par spyod pa dang / legs par rab tu 'byung ba dang / lags par bsnyen par rdzogs par yang 'gyur ro// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi byang chub
